 History of Amalapuram seat The history of Amalapuram Lok Sabha seat is very interesting
 is seat par shuruaati do aam chunaavon (1952 or 1957 loksabhaa chunaav) ko jeetne vaali communist party of india (CPI) vartmaan main apane vajood kii ladaai lard rahi he

 At the same time, TDP has won the victory 5 times
 is seat par 1984 main tidipi, 1989 main congress, 1991 main tidipi, 1996 main congress, 1998 or 1999 main tidipi, 2004 or 2009 main congress ne jeet darj kii

 This preview offer was introduced before the commercial launch of Geofiber Broadband Service

 It is not like a free preview offer

 This offer was first spotted in July 2017

 gujarat kii raajnneeti ke bare main modi virdohi aksar kisi hindu vot yaa prayogshaala kii baat karte the lekin unhen bhi sochna chahie ki aakhir patel asmita wo bhi ek 22 saal ke noujvaan ke netritv main kaise ubhar gai
 That is why it is not a normal political event
 bijepi chup he magar is andolan ko gaur se dekh rahi he
 He is aware that Patel is his biggest and permanent vote bank
 hardik patel kaa imtahaan yahi he ki ve aarakshan se kam par samjhauta karenge yaa aarakshan lekar rahenge
 The problem is that this problem is not for Gujarat
 If this door is opened there, new questions of reservation will arise in front of Prime Minister Modi in Delhi
 supreme court main radd hone ke baad bhi jat aarakshan kaa sawaal samaapt nahin hua he
 The comments gujarat kii mukhyamantri anandiben patel bhi isi samudaay se aati hai jiskaa yuva apni berojgaare or pichhadepan ko lekar sadakon par utraa hua he
 The state government has formed a committee of seven members to talk to these youths
 iskaa netritv swasthya mantri nitin patel kar rahe hai
 There are seven ministers in the Gujarat government
 paanch empi is samudaay se hai
 So why do the rest of the OBC community say from their part to a community that is already prosperous
 thakur samaaj ke netaa alpesh thakur ne kaha he ki obisi maang ke khilaaf anshan karne vaale hai
 Thakur society has more than 30 percent of the 54 percent obcs in Gujarat
 patel samaaj kii bhi sankhya kam nahin he
 17 to 20 percent
 inhen lag rahaa he ki patel aaenge to unka haq maaraa jayega
 Patel youth are also getting support abroad
 times of india kii report ke anusaar england ke patel logon ne united patidaar king naam se ek samooh bana liya he or ve aarakshan kii maang kaa samarthan kar rahe hai
 There is also a stir in the Patel community of America
 isse pehle ki yah maamla global ho jaae local level par charchaa ho jaani chahie prime time main
 After that, the rally in Surat raised the ears of the entire Gujarat
 surat kii raily main lakhon kii sankhya main 22 saal ke is noujvaan ko sunne pahunch gaye
 Before this rally was organized in Ahmedabad, the youth came with 15 to 20 thousand bikes
 ab yah andolan patidaar anamat andolan cameti ke nirdesan main jor pakad chukaa he
 a rally is going to be held in Ahmedabad on August 25, in which lakhs of Patel youth are being claimed
 ham or aap patel samudaay ko samrudh or kaarobaari samudaay ke rup main jaanate hai
 Knowing that he had a relationship with agriculture, but for many decades, seeing pictures of the plush villages of Patels in all magazines and channels, he was convinced that his richness was no match
 patel desh or videshon main gujarat kii samruddhi ke brands ambesader rahe hai
 Their political power is being dominated by population and money
 aisa samudaay aarakshan kii maang karne lage to bahut mehnat kerani pad rahi he ankhon ke aage bane mote parde ko hataane main
 Hardik Patel claims that in the last fifteen years farming has weakened the Patels within the villages
 aabaadi tees pratisht hone ke baad bhi unki sthiti kamazor nazar aati he
 The youth are not getting jobs
 isliye admician or naukari main aarakshan chahie
 Reservation in Gujarati is called Anamat
 ek samay patel netaaon ne obisi aarakshan kaa virodh kiya tha ab obisi darja maang rahe hai
 Right from the social stage, the rise of this 22-year-old youth is telling that nothing has finally happened in politics
 hardik ne gujarat se baahar upi or madhya pradesh main kurmi patel sammelnon main bhi hissaa liya he
 Kurmi in Bihar, Patel or Patidar in Gujarat, says Patil in Maharashtra
 hardik kaa ubhaar sirf patel jati kaa apane liye aarakshan maangana hi nahin balki kheti ke sankat ko bhi saamne laa rahaa he jise ham samrudh gujarat ke prachaaron se bani laal kaaleen ke neeche chipa dete hai
 Patel youths are following Hardik Patel in large numbers regarding reservation
 gujarat me pichley pandrah saalon se lagata rahaa he ki bijepi or bijepi ke baahar narendra modi ke saamne koi doosraa netaa hi nahin he
 Modi's critics wrote that Gujarat has been made the laboratory of Hindutva
 vahaan ke vot kii ek hi pahchaan he hindutv lekin ab unhen bhi apni kitaab phir se padhani chahie ki akhir wo kya baat he ki ek 22 saal ke ladke ke peeche itnaa bada andolan khadaa ho jaataa he
 Patels have also demanded earlier for reservation
 gujarat hi nahin desh ke kai hisson main kai jatiyon ko obisi main shaamil kiya gaya he or shaamil kiye jane kii maang hoti rahi he
 You must remember something about the recent demand for Gujjar and Jat reservation

 ye keemat 6GB + 128GB verient kii he
